## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start Main]) --> CheckMode{find_best_configuration<br/>or single simulation?}
    CheckMode -->|find_best| FindBest[find_best_configuration]
    CheckMode -->|single| LoadData[Load test_data_parquet_path]
    
    FindBest --> IterateConfigs[Iterate feature_set_list]
    IterateConfigs --> SetEnv[Set ML_ALGORITHM_STEP env var]
    SetEnv --> LoadDataConfig[simulation_event_generator]
    LoadDataConfig --> RunSimConfig[run_simulation]
    RunSimConfig --> CalcKPI[Calculate KPIs<br/>within_12hour_count]
    CalcKPI --> WriteFile[Write results to file]
    WriteFile --> MoreConfigs{More configs?}
    MoreConfigs -->|Yes| IterateConfigs
    MoreConfigs -->|No| EndConfig([End])
    
    LoadData --> SimEventGen[simulation_event_generator<br/>limit, skip]
    SimEventGen --> DaskLoad[dd.read_parquet]
    DaskLoad --> IterateRows[Iterate DataFrame rows]
    IterateRows --> ValidateRow{Row valid?<br/>check nulls/NaN}
    ValidateRow -->|No| IncompleteCount[incomplete_row_count++]
    ValidateRow -->|Yes| YieldRecord[Yield test record dict]
    IncompleteCount --> CheckLimit{row_count > limit?}
    YieldRecord --> CheckLimit
    CheckLimit -->|No| IterateRows
    CheckLimit -->|Yes| RunSim[run_simulation]
    
    RunSim --> IterEvents[Iterate sim_event_generator]
    IterEvents --> ParseEvent[Parse JSON query string]
    ParseEvent --> CallETA[eta_lib.get_eta_batch]
    CallETA --> CheckResponse{Response valid?}
    CheckResponse -->|No| SkipEvent[Continue to next]
    CheckResponse -->|Yes| CalcError[Calculate error metrics<br/>error_minutes, error_days<br/>date_diff_minutes]
    CalcError --> AppendSim[Append to simulations list]
    AppendSim --> MoreEvents{More events?}
    SkipEvent --> MoreEvents
    MoreEvents -->|Yes| IterEvents
    MoreEvents -->|No| ReturnSims[Return simulations]
    
    ReturnSims --> CalcMetrics[Calculate KPIs<br/>within_12hour_count]
    CalcMetrics --> CreateOutput[Create simulation_output dict]
    CreateOutput --> WriteJSON[Write JSON to file]
    WriteJSON --> End([End])
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main
    participant SimEventGen as simulation_event_generator
    participant Dask
    participant RunSim as run_simulation
    participant ETALib as eta_lib
    participant FileSystem
    
    Main->>SimEventGen: Call with parquet_path, limit, skip
    SimEventGen->>Dask: dd.read_parquet(path)
    Dask-->>SimEventGen: DataFrame
    
    loop For each row in DataFrame
        SimEventGen->>SimEventGen: Validate row data
        alt Row is valid
            SimEventGen-->>Main: Yield test record
        else Row invalid
            SimEventGen->>SimEventGen: increment incomplete_row_count
        end
    end
    
    Main->>RunSim: Call with sim_event_generator
    
    loop For each test_record
        RunSim->>RunSim: Parse JSON query string
        RunSim->>ETALib: get_eta_batch(event)
        ETALib-->>RunSim: eta_response
        
        alt Response valid
            RunSim->>RunSim: Calculate error metrics
            RunSim->>RunSim: Append to simulations list
        else Response invalid
            RunSim->>RunSim: Continue to next
        end
    end
    
    RunSim-->>Main: Return simulations list
    Main->>Main: Calculate KPIs
    Main->>FileSystem: Write JSON output
    FileSystem-->>Main: Success
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> LoadingData: Start simulation
    LoadingData --> ValidatingRows: Dask read parquet
    ValidatingRows --> ProcessingEvent: Valid row found
    ValidatingRows --> ValidatingRows: Invalid row (skip)
    ProcessingEvent --> CallingETA: Parse query string
    CallingETA --> CalculatingError: ETA response received
    CallingETA --> ProcessingEvent: No response (skip)
    CalculatingError --> ProcessingEvent: More events
    CalculatingError --> ComputingMetrics: Limit reached
    ProcessingEvent --> ComputingMetrics: Generator exhausted
    ComputingMetrics --> WritingOutput: Metrics calculated
    WritingOutput --> [*]: Simulation complete
```
